et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	and let go of the pain, as we have said in the abscess of the liver.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	But in this work there is fear or the patient dies now, or a fistula comes which cannot be healed.
de la mice	Of the mouse.
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent .iij. manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When you cure the disease of the mouse in the way we have said with divisions of cures, and it does not benefit, then there are three manners of cautery that are all good.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	Of which one method is that you make three cauterizations, or four, depending on the length of the mole, according to the figure of the liver cauterization that we have said before.
et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	and do not press your hand on the entire cauterization, and let the patient be mindful of his back.
et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule;	and another method of cauterization is that you scrape the cauterization which has two handles, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder;
et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	and lift the cure which is near the mole, or the patient's cut comes towards the left side, and be the elevations of which you lift the cure according to the cure, according to the length of the body, and the cauterization be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	After putting the two nerves inflamed until the kidneys are perceived from the other side, and then proceed with the fire cauterization, and thus there will be four.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	And if you see, then cauterize the entire cautery to three nerves.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the treatment when he has gotten full recovery for long time, and this is more than the others of the treatments before said.
de ydropisie	De ydropisie.
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Fire cautery does not succeed with an hydropic, except by the manner which is called "asclytes".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you cure it according to the ways we have said in divisions, and your cure does not benefit, then it is necessary that you make four cauterizations around the mouth, and one on the stomach, and one on the liver, and one on the bladder, and two behind the back on the spine, and one in front of the breast.
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	and let the cauterizations be well near the spine of the kidney.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	After leaving the cauterization open to get rid of bad humors for a long time, and not abandoning the patient's cure after the cauterization.
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	and healing would hasten, and the two intentions will be together with God's aid.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The form of the fire cauterization for the belly is the key that we have shown before.
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	and this one for the back is olive-like, according to what it has been placed here before.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the swelling of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are swollen in someone who is dropsical, and are full of yellowish water, it is necessary that you cauterize on the back of the foot between the wrist bone and the pinky finger.
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	and hold your hand with the cauterizer so as not to turn around.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too far in depth, thus the fire would come to a halt, and let the cauter be according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	Then do two cauterizations on each leg, at the tip of the wrist bone.
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	and the long cauterizers, one below the kneecap in front and the other behind, on the leg.
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	and leave the cauterizers there for a long time until the water inside flows out.
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After the healing of other wounds that we have said.
de la menoison	of menstruation
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When a flux of the belly comes from coldness and moisture, as long as the vital and digestive faculties which are in the stomach and intestine are weakened, and cannot be cured by means of treatments.
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	and you see the patient suffering greatly and of great virtue, so make a large cautery on the stomach according to what has been spoken here before about the stomach cautery, by means of circulation.
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	and four small cauterizations around the mouth, subtle as each one is a small nail, and two cauterizations on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et .i. cautere sus chaicun yle, et .ij. petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see the moistors abundant and the patient suffering, then make a cautery on the navel, and one on each vertebra, and two small cauterizations on the stomach near the great one, because the cure is beneficial when there is good aid.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the cure of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When hemorrhoids are in the fundament, one or more, and they are old and are composed of thick, cold, and moist corrupted humors, and they are cured as we have said in divisions, but it does not benefit, so make cauterizations.
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	On top of the spine on the back, that which is entirely below the almond-shaped protrusion and gradually decreasing in a triangular shape, and one fire cautery below the lip two fingers' width.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	And if you think his stomach is chilled, and the meat is not cooked, and one sees his face swelling, then on the face one does a great fire cautery on the stomach, as said before, and another on the liver, and another on the spleen for all the cautery to be done.
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	and leave the cautery open for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treatment let the limb remain until it is healed.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the charnosity which is called "Thelul"
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you cut the ulcer, if the cautery appears to be razor-sharp, then put it all afire on the cut ulcer.
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	and leave your hand there until the cautery comes to the birth of the vein, because the blood will flow.
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	do this once or twice, and if there is much ulceration, then cauterize each one as we have said.
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	after the treatment of ointments benefiting as long as they are healed;
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	and if you cauterize with a great fire on the aloes, it will have greater aid.
de plaie mal curee	of an uncured wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot endure cutting or opening, as we will tell in its place, then comes such a disease that cannot be healed except by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When a fistula comes and is inflamed and discharges pus and corrupted moisture, then you should probe the entire tent-like opening and take note of how deep it goes.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	After the fire that seems rough has cooled, and you apply it to the abscess according to the amount that the liquid has entered, and restart the fire until those corrupted parts are burned, once, twice, or three times, depending on the amount of need.
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	and beware of burning the nerves that are nearby, and the great veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	if the abscess goes to the bladder and into the intestine, be careful of those parts, and do not apply fire except on a well-greased area, and think that it is not perilous.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	after curing the area until it is healed, and if the area is swollen, and the matters are removed over a long time, then know that the area is entirely healed.
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	and if the matters are not removed, know that the bone is twisted, and the bones at the fontanelle are corrupted.
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	and thus as one of those we will say in its place.
de la maladie des reins	From the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When the pain of cold comes to the joints, and from great humidity, and does not take the shape of a woman, then it is necessary that you make a fire cauterization on the joints from one side and the other, at the clavicle cauterization that we have previously mentioned.
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	and if we cauterize it in the middle, there will be three cauterizations in a line, and they will make greater help.
de la vessie	Of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is soft and weak from cold and moisture, so that the patient retains urine, then he makes a cauterization on the part in front of the bladder, where the hair of the pubic region begins, and there is one to the right and one to the left, and each cauterization should be as long as the nose of a pea.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	and do the fire cautery behind the back, or two if you need them;
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	and make the cauterize nails according to the form described before.
de la marris	Of the uterus
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the menses are cold and moist, and do not cease to conceive, and the flowers are corrupted and their ends are late;
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	and when they come, it causes great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	then it is necessary to do three cauterizations around the mouth, as we have said for the caustic of the bladder, and two behind the back;
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	and make the cauterize nails, as we have said.
de la hainche	Of the groin
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When the thick discharges descend to the back of the haunch, and because of this, it moves out of its place, and the sign is that the hip is longer than the other when measured together;
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	et is found the lead of the department view, so it is necessary that you cauterize the patient on the thigh near the armpit with a cautery similar to a circle, and sign in front of the lead around the thigh as it turns, so that the thigh is within the circle;
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	and if the cauteries are such as those with which one has cauterized the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	And if these cauteries are not present, make three large ones on the olive-shaped part, and let the cauteries be as deep as all the bells.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and cure it until it is healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	Of the pain of the groin
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain comes to the thigh near the armpit, and it is due to coldness and moisture, and the patient is cured of what we have said in the division, but the cure does not work, and the disease is ancient:
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	Then it is necessary that you purge the patient of thick, foul-smelling pills or other similar pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	After this, do a fire cautery;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	and the manner of the cautery is according to two manners:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	it means together burning medicines and fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	Fire cautery is according to many manners, one of which is such:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	that you cauterize on the back of the heel three triangular cauteries according to this form, and make good depth and great, and have between each cautery a space as wide as a thumb, and be olive-shaped.
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	one never makes a cautery in the middle of the back of the head, therefore there are four according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you see, then you should cauterize at the circle cautery that we have said before in the dislocation of the back.
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	but make it so that the circles contain all the haunch, and all the spokes of the wheel are burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And that is the manner in which one does it in sciatica, when the pain remains in the haunch and does not reach as far as the hip or as far as the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it comes just to the hip and leg, make two cauterizations there where the patient says that the pain holds them, and one cauterization above the ankle four times, on the left side a little.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	and let the cauterization be cutaneous, and let the spokes of the wheel be burned.
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	and if the patient feels that the pain extends just to two inches of the foot or almost there, then cauterize where they feel the pain three points or four at the cauterization which is called "points".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if necessary, do more to it.
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	and if it is that the pain is below the knee towards the hip, then make a cauterization at the cutaneous or circular cauterization, and take good care in all your cauterizations so as not to leave the cautery too long until you burn the nerves and great arteries, and do not cause more great annoyance and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen many who have had a fire cautery on the ankle of the foot, and left them so that the leg was all inflamed, and the feet also, and it was pierced and corrupted through all the feet.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a purging of the stomach from which he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pains are in two parts together, make a fire cautery in one and in the other, according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the wise men say in the cauterization of the groin, that is how it is done, make such a fire and let it be at the head as big as a walnut or a little less, and let it be between two fingers and let it be from one finger to another the distance of an egg's width.
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	And let the fingers be separated by two parts, and let them also be like hazelnuts, and it should have one good piece of iron well made.
et c’est li forme:	and that is the shape:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	And let it be heated until it is all red and gives off sparks, and then put it on the boil of the patient's groin, and let it be turned above the right side.
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	and let it cauterize once only after the first cauterization, and leave it for three days;
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	and then apply butter, and leave the wound open for a long time;
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the treatment of ointment until he is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Allbuchasium says that we should use little of this fire cauterization for fear of its regard, and if we see few who use it;
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	and yet those are good cauterizations that can be endured by him where it afflicts.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	The burning cauterizations of medicine are those that you make an instrument to fit between the edges of the door, and it should be made of iron or earth for one part to be long, and in the height have two noses, and between each have the quantity of the thickness of a finger.
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and be open on both sides, and come together together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	After put the poultice of the haunch on the lying patient's sound side, and then place your hand most above the poultice of the haunch.
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After gathering between the two circles of hot water that is heated over the fire pot, and let it be an hour's time, and suffer the patient to endure the heat and burning.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	For it also finds a stinging like fire;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	and when the stinging is passed, raise your hand with the instrument and lift the cloth of soft water, and let it be thus three days, and put on butter until that which is black from scorching is removed.
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	and leave it three days so that purging may ensue;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	and this would be the final aid after the treatment of ointments as long as they are healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain has spread to the thigh or leg, make the instrument that holds water according to what you did in the same way.
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	and this is the method of hot water, and I have written it in the treatise on the correction of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkali and hot water, as much of one as the other, and grind them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	where there is a small hole through which the tip of a razor can enter;
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	and place it in another pot well weighted, and place sulfuric alkali and hot water above, so that there will be two layers of powder on top; then you will have it well prepared for your hand.
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	and let it remain thus until the hot water and sediment or weighted pot descend; then take all that water, and pour it on the heat and alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And then it will be very hot and prepared for administering in medical operations and other cauteries.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	For it works as well as fire, and if there are other medicines that one cures well by cauterizing the skin thus with testicle and myrrh and cardamom with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen tells us of a cure where one man was cured of the pain in his hainche and sciatic vein, and he highly praised it, and said that no other cure was made, and he became well only once when this cure was done, and he bathed himself just as it is taught hereafter.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And instruct in this manner that you take green tartrate of fresh and dry earth, and crush it well with a little piece of grease, and apply it on the hip and on the thigh and on the leg where the pain is, and bind it.
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	and leave it for three hours and by the quantity that the patient does not feel any more burning.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then make him enter into a bath until his body is somewhat warmed up, and then make him enter into bed, and the pain will go away altogether and he will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use a fire cauterization on such medications unless it is after the evacuation of the body.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat's hair fires, it helps a lot.
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	and one must make the cauterization in this manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take linen and soak it in old oil, and put it on the hollow between the thumb of the foot and the other one which is called the fleshy part.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	Then take dry goat's hair, and set it on fire until it is coals, and apply it to the wool, and leave it until it is extinguished.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	and do it again in this way, and do not cease to do so until you think by sense that it reaches the hip, and that the pain is ceased.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	and this manner of cauterizing is called "cautere de chievre".
de la dolor dou dos	of the pain of the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether from falling or striking or excessive evacuation or similar signs of cold matter spreading, none of these similarities is worth cauterization, except for that which comes from the infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	It is necessary afterwards that the patient be rid of fetid pills or others similar ones, that one makes them on their back, where the pain holds, three lines marked out in wax, and in each line V cauterizations or more according to the virtue and quantity that the patient can endure.
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	and it should be done with the cauterization called "points".
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	and if you see, make three or four cauterizations at the middle of the cauterizing nail according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	Many times this illness comes to small children, and the signs of its beginning are that they have a narrow, strained look when they wake up, and fear.
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	and you find in the last vertebra of the back and on it the appearance that comes over other vertebrae.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and you see it cured, then cauterize it with the "celcle" cauterization according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	So that the fire cautery may penetrate each part of the spine equally.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, then cauterize around the spine with a fire cautery that pricks 2 lines or 3, and have the points close to one another.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After curing the wound until it is healed according to what we have said, and beware that you do not apply a cautery in a place of giltosity which is near a nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When the pain of joints is due to moistors that are spread throughout each limb of the body, and when pain comes in feet, which the doctor calls "podagre" properly, and when it is caused by cold and medicines cannot cure it, then it is cured by cauterization in this manner:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	Make the heat of the cauterization around the joint of the foot, and let the cauterization be olive-like according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if it is necessary that you prick on the face of the foot, then make a cautery all over the cautery which one calls "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains come to the knees and other joints, and this often happens, then make a cauterization on each knee three times or four from each part, with all the cauterization olive-like;
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	and if you need more, then make more, but do not hold your hand back longer than until the sparks of the iron are burned.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend just to the knee and back, administer the cautery that we have said in its chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if the pains are in the hands, then make points around the wrist two lines;
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	and if there remains no pain at all, then make a puncture on each joint and on the hair of the hand;
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	and if pains come as far as the shoulders or as far as the armpits, then cauterize each part, and make good management of the patient and administer medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you take good care of him and purge phlegm, he will be healed with the help of God.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rupture of the gallstone
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When ulcers come in inguinal areas, and the bowels descend to the groin and it's newly so, then it is necessary that when you see them being cured, do not interrupt him that day.
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	and make him do things that loosen the belly, so that the flux descends from his belly;
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	after that make him sit on his back between your hands, and instruct him to hold his loin cloth until the bowels are restored, and then lift it up to your shoulders, and mark an incision below the ulcer on the bone of the elbow, and all around a sign like the half of a circle above the body.
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Then heat the fire cautery to its form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	as long as he is white and gives senseless statements.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Then reset the bowels to their place;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	and the attendants hold their hands above so they do not return backwards;
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	and work well on the patient's hips, and place under them a cushion and a servant above the hips, and another one above the breast who holds their hands;
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	then place the fire cautery on the sign at the tip of your finger, and hold it steady and straight until you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, so continue again another time until you have reached the bone;
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	and be careful subtly lest the bowels should burst when you do the fire cautery;
que tu ne le brulasses;	lest you burn it;
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and that by this the patient does not die or suffer another evil.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you do not come close to the bone with the fire cautery, your work is worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	And it is necessary that children's cauterizers are subtle according to their size, and for large people also large according to theirs.
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	After three days of treatment, remove the scab from the cauterized area until the inflammation is gone.
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	After treating other ulcers until they are healed, and have the patient lie down on his back for 40 days until the wound is well closed.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And it is necessary that his nails be left long, so that the bellows do not ring out when he is about to go into chambers.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after 40 days, when he wants to get up, have a bandage well made brought to him, and let it be worn for another 40 days.
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	and have good rest, that he not overwork himself and beware of excessive drinking and eating, and too loud shouting.
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	and when he does this teaching then he is completely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say afterwards the treatment of cutting in this chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the running of the belly
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When ulcers come to other bellies and are known, and you see that they do not grow anymore, then the fire cautery is done according to its quantity, and it is burned a third part of the way down.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	after the cure as we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	and none of the ancients have said that one should be cauterized at the fire to three angles according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but first mark the edge of the incision and make a line above the ulcer's width, and another below it, and then insert your hand into the entire cautery channel.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauterization is lighter and more tedious.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of ancient pain in any member
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes to any member, whether from falling or striking, and that pain persists for a long time, and the cure of medicine is of no value, then it is necessary that he be cauterized with the cautery called "points", and the cauterization should be according to the length of the member, its smallness, weakness, and virtue, and its location in terms of torments and pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	if he is healed from the first cautery, it is well;
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	and if he does not, start another cautery on top of it, for such is the custom that one should change to the member that is nearest, so it is necessary that you do cauterizations until the patient is healed.
de meselerie	of menstruation
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The members are aided sometimes by a cauterization with great help, and even the disease that comes from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	Can you not see it being cauterized, take heed if the disease is at its beginning, and if it is cured according to what we have said in the division, and do not descend nor leave anything behind, and you doubt that corruption will spread throughout the entire patient, then make five cauterizations on the head.
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	I move the head forward, and the other [joint] toward the forehead to the end of the hairs.
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	and two above the two horns, and one behind above the haughty person;
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	and let your hand be so still that the cautery comes just to the bone, and stays until the scabs fall off, so that the vapors of the great humors can come out;
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	and cauterize on the mouse according to what it is before.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if the swelling is spread everywhere;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	and it is manifestly inflamed, then it is necessary that you cauterize with the fires of these cauteries which we have said above, and one in the head, and two on the spine of the neck, and six on the spine of the back, and one great one on the scapula and another below, and two on the two shoulders;
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	and II on the sides, and II on the tendons of the back, and I on each joint of the hands and feet, and on the fossae of the hands;
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	and beware of nerves that are on the backside calcanium, lest you burn them;
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	and sometimes make a fire cauterization on the bone of the fingernail, and one on the bone of the stomach, and one on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	And know that when I make more cauterizations, it helps the patient more, and brings greater profit;
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	and know that the patient does not feel any pain from the cauterization as healthy people do, because the body is already quite corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the cautery be great and small according to the members and joints, according to what you will find in the ways of iron.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	Afterward, wash with flour mixed with honey and other cures until he is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When swelling comes to any member and is treated with medicines and oils and plasters, and it is not healed, then one makes cauterizations on the member according to the size and smallness of the member;
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	and let the cautery be slightly inserted into the flesh of the heart;
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then apply ointments as long as they are healthy.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And at times one does a cautery to the hand and foot and back, at the end of the nerve that moves the member, and thus if the swelling is removed.
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	and no one should intervene in this case unless they are familiar with the members and the exit points of the nerves moving through the body.
de albaras	of ulcers
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the disease called "albaras" has taken hold, and the medical art is of no use, then cauterize with a cautery a little bit deep, according to the thickness of the flesh of the heart, until the whiteness is removed, and its color is changed.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	then apply a poultice of flour and vegetables with rose oil and leaves of plantain, and the blood of colander and almond, each one in its part.
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And let them all be together, and be tied with a bandage, and be at rest at the same place until they are healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	the treatment of chance by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When a chancre comes at the beginning, and you see it stop, then cauterize it with the cautery that seems like a circle, all around the border of the chancre.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	And yet the sages say that one makes a fire cauterization in the middle of the sore;
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	and yet it does not seem good to me, for I fear that it will be ulcerated and corrupted, and I have already seen it happen at times;
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	and a more right thing is that he be cauterized around, at the cauterization which is called "circle", as we have said in many cauterizations.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the swelling that cannot be killed
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When someone has a disease which is called "adubelati", and it delays in dying or because of the superfluity that it causes or because of the age of the patient when he is decrepit (that is to say, too old) and he has little blood, or because of the time;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	and you see hastening to die:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	then one cauterizes around with many small cauterizations in pricking;
aprés le laisse ensi.	after that, let it be so.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will hasten to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it piercing through the whole cautery, then heat the cautery with what is called "the form":
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And put your hand in the midst of that disease which is called "adubelati" until the cauteries have pierced the kernel, and be such cauteries that the patient feels them outside in this way that the course of the purgation may be guided.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	Afterward, care for him until he is perfectly healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	the treatment by fire with iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another manner of disease there is which is called "corrodens", and it is nothing else than a wasting away of the member, for it wastes away members just as fire dries out dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this disease in a place that can suffer a burn together with fire, then file the cauterizers small and great, according to what is needed at the place or where the disease is;
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	after that, cauterize all around until you have removed all the corruption, and there remains nothing of it, except for what is corrupted to be cut out.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then leave it for three days, and put on the cauterized areas a poultice with oil until the fire's burn marks are removed, and all corruption is gone.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the healing of ointments brings forth flesh.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if after three days healthy flesh does not form, it is good;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	and if not, then recauterize on what remains of the corrupt places.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this remedy is sometimes cured by medical treatment in place of fire cauterization;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	but all the same fire cautery is of greater aid, and I have already said the treatment of hot remedy in the section:
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	take what you need.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of boils that come to the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Many times it happens that on the feet due to a defect there arises a disease which is called "clos" according to our intention, and it is a big swelling that hurts the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cautery of this disease is according to two manners.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	It is to know fire cautery and water-hot cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	Fire cautery is when you forge a cautery like a awl of beechwood, and it should be made from good iron to the measure that it can pierce through all parts, and have subtle edges.
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	then place everything hot on the nail, and turn your hand entirely around the nail until it comes to the end of the nail.
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	and leave it thus for three days until it begins to putrefy.
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	then make a poultice of wild mulberries crushed with oil, and leave the poultice on all night, and the nail will fall off and be pulled out by its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the joint with oil anointing it until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they are converted by a defect of the body, and it often happens in hands and feet, so you should bring cauterization with hot water;
et est en teil maniere:	and it is in this manner:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	Take a piece of bone or iron, or a quill from a plover, and place it on the nail and the almond, that is to say, small white patches;
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	and place the bone so that it surrounds everything, then put a little hot water on it, and hold your hand well, and press your hand going around so that the edge of the bone comes to the root of the nail, and then find the hot water way deep down to the root;
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	and let the patient suffer a little from the burning of the hot water for an hour;
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	then leave it so, and it will peel off completely to its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Soften one after another, until you have extracted all those inside the body, then treat the sores that produce flesh.
li cure dou trembler	The cure of the trembling
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When some tremble from cold or hernia or quartan fever or another, then you must make four cauterizations on the spine of the back, one between each spine.
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	and one cauterization on the belly, and one above the stomach at the olive-shaped cauterization;
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	so let it tremble, and hasten will be the health of the cold disease.
des pustules puans	of foul pustules
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	Sometimes apparent on the surface of the bathed body or foul pus comes from great corrupted matter.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	it is necessary at first when they appear that one makes a cauterization on each head of the pustule;
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	one subtle cauterization with birch bark or by which the point is seized by fire, or with a long Aristolochia root, or with the lentil-shaped cauterization.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And at the beginning, one cauterizes them according to this manner, and they cannot grow forward anymore, but are broken off the superfluities from which they come, and are healed.
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	but it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when the artery is cut off
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	Many times there occur great hemorrhages of blood from the artery that is cut at the wound that comes to the forefront, or at the incision of an abscess, or at a member's cautery, and similar things.
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	and it is very grievous to staunch.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And yet, when this happens to anyone, if you hasten to place your two fingers on the wound of the vein, and hold it tight until the blood is pacified below your fingers, and no more drops.
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	then set the cauterizers of olive oil on fire, small and large, until they are all red.
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	then take one, either large or small according to the wound and the place where the artery is located, and put the cauterizer on that vein where you are holding your fingers, and hold the cauterizer there until the blood is stanched.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement .i. autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it bursts forth when you lift your fingers from the vein, and the cauterization has cooled, then take quickly one other of the cauterizations that are in the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	And do not cease to perform these one after another until the blood is exhausted.
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	and beware that you do not burn the nerve which is below, and that no other harm comes upon the patient;
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	and know that when blood flows out of the artery, one cannot well repress it even if the artery is large, unless it is done by one of the four methods we have said:
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	or by cauterization, or by extracting it when it is not yet treated, or by strong binding with thread, or by medicines applied which have the power to stop blood;
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	and be tied and held tightly in place.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever thinks to stanch blood by binding tightly with cloths or putting hot things on it, or other similar things, will not profit unless the cauterization is not good.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if this happens to anyone and they do not have a mirror or medicine present, then one should put their two fingers on the wound of the vein as we have said, and stretch it tightly until it is stopped above the wound and above the vein;
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	and do not move it, but moisten with cold water frequently until the blood is congealed and thickened and stopped.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	and make inquiries ahead of those that have need of cauterizations and medicines.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book of surgical cures
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We have told you in the first chapter about all disease where it is necessary to cauterize with fire or with hot medicine, and the methods, reasons, and forms of cauterizations.
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	and I have placed that chapter at the beginning of the book, and I will proceed in this chapter by the same way for those who find it more readily what they desire.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And therefore as I begin this, dear friend, you should know that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first of the cauteries, and for that reason it is necessary to take greater caution.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the work of this chapter, there is often evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things;
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you not to undertake folly.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many ways of people come into cures.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	those who are so tormented by their disease that they would die quickly because of the suffering they find in their illness and the greatness of their malady.
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	and one should be afraid of these things.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	And from these ones who give you sense and say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	Wait, I am healed";
et li maladie est despitouse.	and the disease is spiteful.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	It is not fitting that you consent to those who come to you with this manner, but put more great caution in your honor than in your covetousness, and do not foolishly but wisely from what you are certain of and can take and gain.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	and use prediction and indication in the treatments of your sick to whom salvation may be converted;
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	and this will help you to acquire good reputation, and glory, and praise.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Very dear son, May Our Lord give you good understanding and straightness, and if you wish to be filled with the holy inspiration of His hand, Amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Now I have finished this chapter by dividing it into chapters, according to what is before the chapter of cauterizations, which I have divided from the beginning up to here, so that you may find more easily what you will need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	from the full head with water
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	Know that this disease comes often to children during childbirth, and when the midwife constrains the child's head too tightly.
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	and sometimes it comes from an unknown cause because one doesn't know.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	And I never saw this disease outside of children, and all those that I have seen died suddenly.
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	and for this reason it seems to me that I should stop working on such cures.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	And I saw an infant whose head was full of water, and the head grew bigger each day until it could no longer be borne.
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	and the moisture was so great that it killed him, and this moisture is gathered under the bone above the spine, between the skull and the bone.
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	and the works are such that if moisture is between the bone and the muscle, and abscesses are small, you should cut a wide incision in the head.
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	and it should also be as long as two of us, as long as the moisture runs.
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	and see to the shape of the spatula-like thing:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai .ij. fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more swollen and the abscesses are larger, then make two incisions in the shape of a cross, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	And if the moisture is below the bone, and you see signs that each part of the head's commissure is open, and the water jumps forth greatly when you press it with your hand from within, and this does not respond to you.
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	so you should cut three incisions into the head in this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after incising, extract all moisture away.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	After binding the incisions with cloths and powders, and applying wine and oil, and leaving it like that until the fifth day;
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	Then loosen it, and treat the wound with tenting and ointments, and let the head be strained to the same extent, and then let the patient eat dry meat without moisture until the member is comforted and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	And another way of incising is to look at where the swelling of the abscess lies, and the gathering of water.
car aucune fois est elle devant;	for sometimes it is before;
aucune fois derrier;	sometimes behind;
aucune fois en destre;	sometimes to the right;
et aucune fois en senestre.	and sometimes on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	Cut then there where the abscess opens, and the filling of water, and make it according to what you can do.
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	and be careful that you don't cut the artery;
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	and let flow a vein of blood, so that the patient may die from loss of blood and evacuation of moisture.
de reume	of the joint
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les .ij. arteres.	When it happens to someone with a disease called "catarre" in the eyes or at the liver, and the disease is ancient, and medical treatment does not help, then the last resort is fire cauterization, by cutting off the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	It is then necessary, when you see them cut, that the patient put their head back;
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	after the wound is rubbed with a rough cloth until the arteries appear, then pull the patient's neck all the way down to the cloth;
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	Then look where the vein lies, and the ears of one side and the other are after the ears, and they are not responded.
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Then mark the ears with a stain, then cut one and the other with a sharp instrument of two parts, so long as the vein comes up to the bone, and let it be by the length of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com .ij. dois au traver.	And if you see, push the spatula under the artery and cut above it, cutting just like two fingers across.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, blood will spring forth continuously upwards.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	And if the artery does not open to the sense, then it is necessary that you measure the quantity of space of three fingers, then mark with a stain and make up to the bone;
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	and as much blood as is necessary to put forth if it is six cubits, and by chance a little more or less, according to what the patient can bear, and the replenishment of the artery;
puis regarde la plaie:	Then look at the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	if it remains on the bone's point of the syphac, then cut what abscesses do not come there, and then strain the wound and tie, and the ointment treatment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	of migration
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When ancient migration comes, and acute catarre, due to excessive moisture of tears and heat in the temples and old-fashioned foreskin and similar things, and all medical treatments by various methods of medicine do not help him, then we extract the arteries from the temples and cauterize them, as we have counted.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	The manner of extracting them is that the patient makes his hairs on his temples recede, and pays attention to the artery that opens in the temple, for it opens well by its pulsation, and is more readily responded to than in some men who are too cold.
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	And if it is responded to, then the patient tightens his neck with some cloths, and then rubs the joint with a rough cloth, and raises the joint in warm water until the artery appears clearly.
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	Then take the spatula which has this shape:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	Then scrape the skin lightly until you come to the artery, then pinch it high up and carefully separate it from the layers that are below each part.
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	And if the artery is thin, then turn it at the tip of the needle, and cut from that part according to the quantity of two joints.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	Since she is not cut, the blood does not flow at all.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	And drain the blood of six cups, up to three;
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	and if the artery is large, it's necessary that you tie it in two loops with a strong double thread of silk, so that no clot forms before the wound closes, and blood flows freely.
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	then remove the excess that is between the two loops at the same time, and then, if you see fit, use a cutellated cautery to cauterize the area up to the bone until the ligaments are cut.
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	and that is the main work if the patient has no fever and is of warm constitution.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	For cauterization helps to end moisture:
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	therefore it is of greater help for moistures.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	Or, when extracting arteries, one should fill the place with old cotton and put a well-made tent over it.
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and when they are freed, one should take care of dry medicines that produce flesh and tents, until he is healed.
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	and if there is no blockage of the artery as long as you work on it, then hasten to cover with a cauterized cloth, or apply vitriol to the place and strain it in your hand so that the blood is stopped.
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	and if you don't have that present, then put a poultice on the place as long as the blood is frozen, and apply cold water to the place until the bleeding ceases, and strain it as needed.
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	and what is more effective and lighter in the extraction of the artery is that you cauterize the vein with this cauterizing blade cutting into two parts, but the blades should be well spaced to withstand their heat longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the cuts are too dense, they retain less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	And it should be that between the two knives there is a space of about an inch, and then when you have signaled to close the two levers, and then apply the hot iron on top until it reaches the bone, and cut the vein in two parts.
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	and let them be separated between the two shoulders because it is not solidified by this fire cautery from end to end;
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	and that is the shape of the cautery:
des larmes	of tears
