de la routure dou syfac	of the rupture of the gallstone
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The events of this rash are caused by the section that comes from the sweat gland, or the extension above the belly in the area of the groin, for which the intestines descend into one of the testicles;
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes:	and this rash is either from sweat or from extension above it, and there are two ways these things come about due to various causes:
ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	or from percussion, or jump, or bellowing, or lifting a heavy load, and similar things;
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	and the signs when it's from sweat gland extension are that they appear gradually over a long time, and do not come suddenly;
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	and the abscesses are even down to the very bottom, because sweat gland pressure pushes out the intestine.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs are when it is of the section of syphilis, which brings sudden pain at the beginning, and there are diverse abscesses appearing underneath the skin close by, and this is because of the issue from the intestine and the body being drained of the syphilis.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the abscesses burst with the intestine, and are retained there, and cause great pain to suffer in the patient, especially when it is pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these iron treatments, there is fear, for which one must take heed.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the manner of the work is that you instruct the patient to push the intestine back into its place with his hand inside the wound, if it can be inserted;
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	Then be mindful on his neck. Between your hands, and lift the hips;
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	Then stretch the skin above, and cut all the skin of the scrotum to its length;
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	Then push the leaves of the bandage into the wound in a way that you need to open it, and be such that the eye can come out;
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	Then scrape off the suppurated flesh that is under the skin of the scrotum, until the white suppurated flesh is exposed from all sides;
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	Then insert your two fingers into the space where the scrotum is, between the white suppurated flesh that is under the skin of the scrotum, and between the second suppurated flesh;
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	and then move your right hand into the skin of the scrotum, and lift the white suppurated flesh up to your left hand, and lift the testicle towards the belly;
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	and instruct the attendant to stretch the cloth upwards, and loosen what is above the knot.
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	and seek at your hands if there is any inflamed or whitish swelling in the intestine; and if you find anything, bind it to the belly beneath.
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	then take a needle where there is thick thread made of nine threads, and sew it in the back part of the swelling which is after the skin of the scrotum;
aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	after the cutting, then trim the strings that appear from the sons, as long as there are four threads.
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	then gather them together one upon another in the shape of a cross, and bind the swelling, which we have said is beneath the skin of the scrotum, with a strong band of two parts.
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	then envelop the strings of the sons, and bind them strongly with two parts, so that no vessels that nourish them can enter inside, lest an abscess should not come.
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	and put the ligament above accordingly with the first long ligament two fingers' breadth below the key of the joints.
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	and after that, all the others according to the roundness that the egg carries;
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	then cut in the part that is below the skin of the joints, until the blood flows and the bowels move, as we have said before.
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	then apply moistened wool in oil to wounds, and put it on the joints, and apply the ligament that we have said.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the white syphilitic discharge that we have said is cauterized after incision, out of fear of blood dismemberment.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	For this often happens, and leave the ligament until it pulls itself loose;
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	and if it does not come loose, then raise warm water and put it on what we have said, until it comes loose;
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	then treat the wound with another treatment, until it is completely healed.
de hernie carnouse	of a fleshly hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this recipe I never saw anyone who dared to perform the treatment by fire.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancient ones say that it is made like the twig that is together with the vine, in such a manner that you tie the vessels, after the cutting above and lightly below.
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	then cut into me, and treat the abscess of those who work, until the vessels bleed.
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then cure it as we have said, until he is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	In some cases a rupture comes in the groin, as we have said, and opens the swelling.
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	and do not let any of the intestines come out through the anus, and if they do come out, it is little, and repair them every hour.
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	and yet if he stays too long in this point, the wound or boil grows, until the intestines come out.
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	and this happens through the extension of the boil which is in the groin, as we have said, because it is extended, then softened and swollen, and opens.
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	and the cure is by fire cauterization, as we have said before;
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	and sometimes it is cured in this manner:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	and it is that the patient lies thus on his back between your hands, then cut the swelling of the rupture to the width according to the quantity of three fingers.
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	and then extract the pus that is below the skin and that follows, then take the raw flesh and place it on the apparent surface of the pus.
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	and press it into the deepest part of the belly, then cut the two apparent surfaces of the pus on the top of the raw flesh, and cut one and the other.
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	then extract the top of the raw flesh, and do not cut or stretch any other thing from the pus, as I have shown you in the cure of the gout of the intestines;
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	Then the treatment by wound treatment.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cauterize the sons, so defile and cure the wound, until it is sound.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The syphilitic discharge is constricted and has no appearance in the rupture, and the cauterization is more useful in this place, and closer to salvation.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of the softening of the skin of the intestines
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	The skins of some men are often softened in many places because the humors that are inside are softened, and it is to be seen.
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	and it is necessary when one wants to cure him that one makes the patient lie down on his back and scrapes off the softened skin from the natural skin.
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	Then bring together the two lips at a seam, and if you see fit, sew first the excess of the softened skin at three seams or four firmly.
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Then scrape between the seams and treat the wound like others until it is healed, and let the thread go.
dou chastrement	The punishment
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	Know that castrations are esteemed in our law, and therefore it would please me not to speak of them at all in this book.
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	and it is necessary only for two reasons:
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	When one is ill-treated in his own sight to answer what is asked when it is demanded of him, and in his own sight to heal.
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	and the other, because we often need to use correction on certain beasts to help us, such as goats and sheep and goats and other beasts.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	I say then that correction is done in two manners:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	or by attraction or by splitting.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	In that which we do by attraction, we make the beast sit in hot water until the sinews are softened and relaxed.
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	then taking them with your hand, until they are restored and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille:	Of the correction of size:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	it is necessary that you stretch the beast, and press the skin of the sinews to your left hand, then tie the suspender, and strike each joint one stroke, when you have well separated them;
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	and I leave no poultice of dry sulfur and the subtle sulfur which is on the vessels;
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	and this manner of correction is worse than that which is done by attraction, because at the attraction something remains from the testicles, and for this reason the beast desires lust;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	then treat the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	of hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	Hermafrodite is according to two manners in men:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	one manner is that between the two testicles appears also like the figure of a woman's nature, or it has hair, and sometimes in court the urine.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other manner is in women, and has on the thumb also like a penis and two testicles.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	And the care of man and woman is that you cover all the joined parts and treat them as other wounds;
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	in the second manner, men from whom urine jumps through the skin of the testicles, have no care.
de la tentigene	of the tenting
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	A figuration is attached to the natural part on the skin, as long as it is too ugly to see.
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	and some women have it just as big as a hand, and that's what it cures.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	You should paint the excess of the figuration on your hand or nails, and trim it lightly;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and don't go too far in cutting, lest blood comes forth from it, and then the cure of another cure is needed until he is healed.
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	and to another mark that appears on the mouth of the marris, and it's filled in, and by chance it jumps forth, and is according to the likeness of a cow, and for this reason they called it "disease of the cow" in olden times.
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	If you need to reset it, as we have said the remedy, and the treatment until it is healed.
de erratique	of the erratic one
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	It is errant if the natural condition of the woman is not perceived, or if the pustules are small;
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	and it is natural by birth, or an accident by disease that has come to be;
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	or it is due to a joined bone, or subtle abscess, or swelling, and it happens in the middle, or in the sides, or below, or wherever it may be;
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	and hindering conception, and childbirth, and by chance having flowers to have;
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	and the knowledge of this is through the look of the gallbladder.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the swelling is nearby appearing, seek it at the shoulders or in the breast.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	If it is a subtle abscess and it is close to two bones, then hasten and cut thus:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	put your two middle fingers together, and the woman should be on her back, spreading her legs;
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	then bring the two bones into form, until the subtle abscess is reduced, and cover the swelling;
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	then take linen, moisten it in oil, and place it on the bone, and have the woman sit at home each day, so that it may not unite.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the fistula is hard and narrow, it is necessary that you cover it with a spatula similar to a myrtle leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	If the swelling is of flesh-born origin, then suspend it at the incision and cut.
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	and have the medicines that stay blood, such as, dragon's blood, frankincense, and together with many eggs.
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	then apply a bandage of linen wide, so that the wound cannot close.
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	and thus be for a long time, and apply a tent of dry linen.
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then be cured by other treatments until you are healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when new flesh comes in the margins, it is necessary to cover it according to this manner, unless it is enchanted abscesses.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For an enchanted abscess that is in the margins, one should not touch with fire.
des emorroides	of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Varicose veins are openings of veins that have become accustomed to being without constraint, and when varicose veins are old they become ulcerous.
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	and we have said in the section what resembles them, and the signs, and I will say here those that receive a cure.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I diagnose that hemorrhoids and piles, when they are deeply embedded in the rectum, and do not respond to sensation, except perhaps through medical treatment by fire.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those who are at the mouth of the rectum, which can be felt, are those that can be cured.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	It is necessary then that you put the woman in a cold house, then cauterize the ulcer with tongs, and cut into its roots, then powder on medicines restraining blood, such as dragon's blood and frankincense, and similar things.
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	then bind his feet to the appearance of an hour, then put it in cold water;
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	and if blood is discharged and comes forth, then make it sit in a decoction of sumac and green apple bark and galls and similar things, and then take barley flour, mix it with honey and egg white, and make an ointment to apply on his back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it stays, it's good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	If not, then make him wear poultices on the back and around the breasts so as not to hurt them;
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	then take linen, and soak it in plantain juice or in elderberry juice with old wine, and apply it to the place.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess has healed, then treat the wound with ointment until it is clean.
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	and that which is called "albathir" is red and is similar to an ashen head, then it should be covered as I have said before with oil.
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then continue with the treatment until they are healed.
des apostemes de la marris	of the womb apostemes
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many kinds of abscess come to the marriage bed, such as syphilis and stony abscesses and herpes and boils and swellings and fistulas and hemorrhoids and hot abscesses, and many other diseases that I have mentioned in the division.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	It is necessary therefore that I describe in this treatise the hot abscess that occurs in marriage, which is not like the abscesses that surround a boil.
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	and if you wish to know the operation of iron, observe whether the abscess is warm at the beginning of its appearance, and full of heat and fever, and if it turns red so that you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Then do not hurry to pierce, but let it subside until the pain is alleviated.
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	and then make the patient sit on a stool, and have two small stools or he leans on, and support himself with his back and bring his feet together away from the leg.
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	and let his thighs be spread apart, and put his arms under his knees, and tie them well with a good bandage.
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	Then follows the ball game towards the right side, and there are placed the instruments with which one works at the mouth of the marriage, from which afterwards comes the form.
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	and it is necessary that when you are about to place this instrument there, you mark the first line straight so as to know the depth of the marriage, so that what enters into the instrument does not go too deep and does not harm the patient.
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	and if the instruments are larger, it is necessary to cover the depth of the marriage with cloths, so that the instruments do not cause harm.
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	and it is necessary that he puts the rim of the instrument above and holds the instrument.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	And when the abscess opens and one works it with a soft hand, then it is necessary to cover it at the head, above the collarbone.
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	and when the bowstring is empty, so you should put damp cloths soaked in rose oil or green oil into the wound;
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	and put the cloth far from the wound at the bottom of the marsh, and put one above the marsh and on the clean linen dampened in water or cooked mallows;
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then the healer after two days of ointment according to this, until it is healed;
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	and sometimes lift the marsh and the wound by washing with water and honey, and then with water or lily roots and long aristolochia cooked;
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	then reapply the ointment.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is placed in a sling, then it's necessary that you avoid cooking with iron, but cure it as we have said in the division.
de l’enfantement	of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	It is necessary first at the bedside that she knows the figure of natural childbirth, and the signs are such when you see the woman descending below and desiring to give birth.
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	Then the children hurry to get out.
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	Then you know that this childishness is according to natural form, and the issues beneath his head, and the second joints with it.
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	and when you see these signs, then it is necessary to gently press his belly so that the child may come out soon.
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	for when he descends above his head, then the second joints are with him, and the excesses of his superfluities are purged by good purification.
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	and this one that comes otherwise does not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	For sometimes it comes above his feet, or above the chest or head, or in his hands, or above his belly, or somewhere else, and is converted by chance on his neck, and by other bad shapes.
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	So it is necessary for the ball to be wise and subtle in these things, and beware of error and deception, and I will show you all the shapes how one should help him.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	If the child comes out on its head by natural issue, and the woman gives birth in travail, and the virtues of it are weak, then make it sit on a stool, or women hold it.
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	and its natural excretion of oil or fenugreek is cooked, and then pour the bail between its two navel strings, which is the form.
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	and split the afterbirth, and cut to his navel string until the moisture that is inside comes forth.
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	and paint the woman's belly until the child descends, and if it does not descend, then it is necessary to purgative the woman with fenugreek mixed with sesame oil.
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	then make her press and strain with condensation, and keep her mouth and nose for an hour.
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	so now the child is still.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	And if the two hands are too far apart, then you must bring them together gradually little by little;
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	and if they cannot enter, then the woman should sit on the siege, and lift her feet up high;
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	then remove the siege from the ground, and hold onto the woman so she does not fall while standing;
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	and if the hands cannot enter and the child dies, then cut open the hands with the knife that is placed beforehand, and extract the child, and bring it back into place;
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	from the birth of the child on his feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the child comes out onto its feet, then it is necessary to raise it up high;
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	and then turn it little by little until it is even;
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	then take the foot and stretch it little by little.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	Can he jump as far as his thighs, then command her to bend down, and make her stretch out with condishion;
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	If it jumps away, then may God will.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it does not come forth as we have said, then turn it slowly and carefully until it is according to the natural figure.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then it will be easy.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	And if it doesn't come away as we have seen, then take mastic of the elder, and oil of sassafras, and melted gum, and grind all in a mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	and put it on the natural of the woman inside and outside this ointment, then make her sit in cold water down to below the ribs.
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when she is moistened below, put a collyrium of myrrh on it, and put it underneath, and let her have an hour.
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then make her sit on the stool, then make her cough and strain her mouth and nose, and lightly palpate her belly, for the child now jumps.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	of the issue of the child from its knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the child comes in this form, I put it into its mother's hands little by little.
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	Then be sure on his neck, and the feet hang down below, and be supported above the bed;
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	and fold his hands little by little, and then take hold of the hands above the belly, and lift away the pillows below, until it is aligned down;
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	and if the child does not cry out, take his feet and shape them well, then shape the belly upwards, then put your hands in;
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	and rock the child little by little;
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	and instruct the woman to take hold until the child comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	of the issue of the child which comes out with one hand holding onto something.
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	it is necessary to contrive to bring back the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	if one cannot bring it back, then have the woman get up and go;
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	if she cannot walk, then make her lie down on the bed, and lift away her legs well;
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	Then administer the muscle-like thing which I have counted.
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	and if it does not give birth, then make her sit on the siege, and then study to bring back the hand;
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	and shape it according to its natural figure, and make it protrude, and command her to grasp as the child emerges forward.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	of the issue of the child from its neck, and having spread its hands, and its face turned towards its mother's back.
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	It is necessary that the nurse hold his hand, then turn him a little bit by little bit, and gently ease him;
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	and when he is equal, then put on the muscle-like thing of aloes and oil, as we have said, and command her to move slowly.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	and when you have done this, then make her sit on the siege, and command her to grasp;
et la fai esternuer.	and make it protrude.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	of the same manner for all the afterbirth.
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When he comes forth in this way to the entire joint, then cut the joint at your fingernail, until the moisture is drained.
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and if the child bites its face and neck, so that the skin breaks open and it is not retained, and the child will die;
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	then put the child inside until you have placed him as it is fitting, and instruct the woman to take hold of him sometimes:
adonques si istra legierement.	then if he stretches lightly.
de l’issue des gemelz	of the issue of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	Know that triplets are often born, and sometimes four or more.
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	and this is not an unusual thing, nor does it happen rarely.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	Twins are an unusual thing, and they do not live if only two can be named;
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know that they are multiplied, and they are divided by the placenta which divides them, which is attached to the womb;
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	and sometimes they issue naturally just like one from above, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they are grievous, then follow the cure as we have said, and be subtle in the treatment, and do quickly and lightly what it does;
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and do thus as it is worth for one's salvation.
de plusors enfans	of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	There are no more than fifteen days formed in the first, second, third, fourth, fifth, sixth, or seventh month, and they are all shaped like children by the measurement of glorious wisdom, and it is necessary that the doctor knows everything about this, for similar things may happen to him.
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	and do according to what is necessary.
de l’enfant mort	of a dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you cure the woman after a stillborn child or miscarriage, as I said in the division, and it does not come forth, and you are compelled to work by hand;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	so that you know whether the woman is of good virtue, and has no accident or is not afraid of death;
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	If it is necessary that the woman be seated on her back, and have her feet inclined downward, and her legs lifted.
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	and the midwife should apply a thread of two parts to the mother's bed, or she is tied to the bed so that she will not be disturbed in giving birth to the child.
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	then moisten the mother's mouth with oily liquid made from aloes and fenugreek and flaxseed, then anoint her hands with these oils and medicinal liquids.
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	then put them into the mother lightly, then have her lift up or push out the afterbirth that is conducive to this, and take care that the child descends onto its head.
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	if the afterbirth comes out into her eyes or neck or mouth or palate or under the beard or in the forehead or near the ribs, and if it descends on its feet, then set it or push it away from the sides.
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	and it is necessary that he hold the ligature in his right hand, and put the bandage between the fingers of his left hand, and tie all his hand lightly, and place the ligature in any of those places that we have said, until it comes to the empty thing;
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	and this is the form of the ligature:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	then place it opposite another ligature, or a third one if you need it, so that the extractions are equal;
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then stretch it evenly by moving from one side to the other, so that there may be movement, and the ligatures are tight enough to hold the movement, as is its form:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if a part remains, then anoint the bail with some oil, and tie it in that part, and draw the other part;
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	and if there is none left, then place this ligature or more above, and do so until it all comes out altogether.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes before the other, and he cannot bring it back because of the constriction, so you must envelop it with a cloth, until it becomes entirely.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	Then wrap the bandage around the joint of the foot or at the ankle, and thus you must do in the other hand, and with both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the child's head is large and it is strained in the birth, or it has a sharp edge assembled, so you must push the spatula-shaped spine between your two fingers, and make the head and extract the water.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	or you should cut it with the instrument which is called "almidach", because the shape comes with the instruments or chapter that follows this one.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and thus do the same if the child has a great natural head.
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and then pull the bones apart with pincers, and if the head jumps out and it strains at the forceps, so that they are split, until the liquids which are in the issue come forth.
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if she cannot come out, so cut her apart into sections as you can.
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	and if he is swollen in the belly or below the ribs, then it is necessary that you make a hole so that the moisture runs out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the child is on its feet, then the traction is light, and the direction towards the mouth of the womb is light.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if he is strangled in the belly or at the chest, then it is necessary that you loosen him from the wrapping cloth on your hand.
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and make a cut in the belly or the chest, until the moisture which is there flows out.
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	and if the other limb is pulled off and the head remains, then put the bail's hand into the farthest part of the wound, and pull it to the mouth of the wound.
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	then put in one or two fingers and pull him forth.
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	and if the mouth of the wound is constricted because of hot abscess that has come there, then it is not necessary to struggle, but rather prepare things moist and greasy.
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and the plasterer should prepare ointments, and six in softening and moistening waters.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the child is on its side, and you can put it straight, then plaster as we have said in a living child;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if one cannot, then take it apart piece by piece, and leave nothing of the second part.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, then plaster as we have said in abscesses that come to the swelling;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and if there comes forth blood flowing, it should be put into water restraining it, and another plaster applied.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman whose womb had contained a dead child, then she consulted with another about that one, and rejected the dead one.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, an abscess came forth in her mouth, and swelled so much that it burst open, and began to cause great turmoil.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to the treatment, and I thought for a long time, and could not stop the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied a plaster with strong traction, and one bone came out, and after some days another.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was very surprised, because the womb has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	So I thought that it was the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I wish the wound, and in bringing together several bones, until the woman was in a better condition;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and the woman stayed thus for a long time, and then occasionally came forth a little pus from the wound;
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I do not recall this chapter being opened except for this reason that when the master finds an unusual thing he knows how to put it right.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	of returning the marrow to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	Next comes the shape of the pressure point, by which one reads the books;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	and at two turns on both sides of both shoulder joints.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	However, the combs should be more subtle than the restricting one, and should be made of ebony or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and the mouth of the fist should be about two hands wide, and the edge of the trees one palm and a half long;
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and between the two joints there should be about half a palm or a little more of space;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	and these two joints are joined in the mouth of the fist to open when one turns the two combs.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, made more subtle and light-like, should be fashioned from boxwood or ebony, according to the appearance of pincers;
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	and have two notches, just like you see, one palm long and two inches wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	and when you see the opening of the uterus at all instruments, make the woman sit on the bed, her feet spread apart and her legs open wide, then insert the two notches together into the uterus, and hold the head of the instrument under between her hips;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then work your hand on the instrument, just like you have done with pincers evenly, according to the amount that you see opening the mouth of the uterus, until the patient makes it as she wishes.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	These instruments are all mounted and have multiple shapes;
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	and when the mirrors are prepared, then the work is all the more hasty and higher for men due to their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not despise the instrument that you have prepared, for its necessity is not excusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the afterbirth is retained at childbirth, then you must instruct the patient to retain her urine and then have it stirred with conditions, and hold her hands to her mouth and nose;
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	and if she does so because of that, well it is.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, then I take a poultice, and make a patch or covering, and put herbs in it that can open the mouth of the womb, such as calamus, rue, anise, chamomile, cascioline, and centaury;
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	all these herbs or some of them being cooked or steeped in water above the fire;
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	then place a cloth or patch on the pot, and the other end in the mouth of the womb, and tighten it so that the fumes come inside the womb;
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	Then let it be estranged, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the secondine heats up quickly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if it remains after this cure and is not fully healed, instruct the nurse to moisten her left hand with sesame oil or musk mallow of hawthorn, and then apply it in its natural state, and ask for the second time.
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and when she has found it, take it and stretch it little by little correctly, so that the hairs do not hinder the extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	but make it move slightly to the right and left, and then draw it.
si venra et se desaerdra.	and so it will come and become disarranged.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the mouth of the hair is too narrow, we have said the treatment for estrangement and the fumigation of herbs;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if she does not follow all that we have said, then be careful not to make a mistake while drawing.
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary that what is at the mouth of the marriage, you tie to the thigh of the woman, then anoint with ointment four-pharmacologist.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	if it will permit and restore, and comes forth;
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	but nevertheless, when she permits this, a bad smell comes to the stomach and head, and hurts the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	So it is necessary then to perform suitable fumigations for that:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	no ancient has proven the effectiveness of fumigation with dandelion and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The form of the instrument with which one fumigates the woman to retain the flowers and the secondine is this:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it seems like a chain, and one places the head subtly in its natural state, and the large joints above the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and let the fumigations be on the coals, and the lice until it is wasted, and then start another.
de percier lou fondement	of piercing the foundation
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who do not have the foundation pierced, but it is stopped by subtle signs.
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	So then it is necessary for the midwife to pierce that subtle sign at its due time, and not let it be pierced by sharp instruments, and guard the position so she does not touch it.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then apply a moist linen cloth in vinegar and oil, then treatment with ointment until it is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will not stop, put a cord of flax into the wound and let it stay for many days, and be removed when the child wants to go to chambers.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And sometimes this stopping occurs suddenly in a wound or abscess;
si covient coper celui soudement:	So then it is necessary to cover that sudden swelling:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	if it be cured, as we have said about the knot of flax.
de la fistule dou fondement	of the fistula of the foundation
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas that come from below the foundation are swelling, and grow larger than those that come from above the foundation or in the space of two parts, if there is one fistula or more.
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	and when that swelling is old, so it works, and with more moisture awakens white or subtle pus, and sometimes these abscesses persist;
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	and are accompanied by this, that it either empties out or vents itself when the patient makes an evacuation, and possibly jumps into one's face.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And if these abscesses penetrate just to the bladder, and just to the middle of the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	and reach just to the junction of the buttocks, and just not the knee.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one knows that the abscess persists at the fundament, and does not persist:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and is that you push your index finger or fundament, and push in a subtle needle of iron or steel into the abscess when there is no twistiness.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if it has twistiness, then push in a subtle awl or horsehair, until you feel the awl or hair at your finger.
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and he does not come with a perforation or ejection of wind or pus, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	know that it does not penetrate.
si te haste dou curer.	if you hasten to cure.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula is pierced all the way to the bladder or the urethral canal, if it jumps with urine, and cannot be healed by medicines.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it is pierced just to the joint of the hip, then the tendon comes right up to its place;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	if there is no twisting and the cause of the pain surrounds it, then it goes to the back, and no medicine or poultice by anointing is worth;
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and in these Persian fistulas there is no cure other than hard work, and vanity of foolish physicians who meddle with them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In one that is not Persian and not old, there is hope of recovery by iron, as I have proven, and it is that the patient lies between your hands on their back;
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and let the patient's legs come down to his hips, and have his hips inclined towards his belly;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	then pitch a tent of clay or if there is twistiness, as long as you know where the tent comes from.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the patient feels it around the foundation, then you should place your two fingers there, if then the tent has pierced.
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	and be discovered where you feel between your finger and the flesh or fat, then know that it is purulent;
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	if one does not work on it, it cannot be healed.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	One says that some can indeed be healed, but this happens rarely;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the help one gives is to cauterize the subtlety of the abscess according to the width of the fistula, as it was said before;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	and make the poultice hot in the fistula, until it comes to the foundation.
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and do this twice or three times, until you know that these charred fragments are burnt, which are similar to a bird's feather.
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then apply oil from moist tents in butter, until that charred fragment comes out, then apply ointment anointing the wound and closing it.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If it is thus healed, it is good.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If this, otherwise it cannot be healed;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if the tent goes in and does not pierce all the way to the doot which is at the foundation, and there is a dense covering of char or of flesh between your skin and the tent, and you see the fistula on the surface that closes the covering of gold.
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	so cut at the beginning of the fistula, and put afterwards before the tent, and then apply the cauterization after, until it comes to the top of the tent.
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	and will be freed the tent, and falls;
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	then define those deformed nails that seem like a bird's feather, and leave none remaining.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the blood increases, and cuts between you and the work, then cauterize with fire or medicine again.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cauterization brings together two things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	that is to say, the burning of these deformed nails, and the drying up of blood and the evaporation of moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then treat the wet tents with butter or bruised herbs, until the pus flows out, and let the burned nails fall into the pus;
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then cure the wound of the swarming sores that form hard flesh, and are the dried medicines.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, then it is healed and does not come back.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if the fistula comes all the way to the bottom of the fundament, and is distant from the body, then insert your finger into the fundament and feel around.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you feel the tent and between two is the cloth or the syphac or nails, where it is close to bursting, except there are fires that go by faith and hope, through the administration of one of the three manners:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	You cauterize it as we have said, or you cut to the bone, or if you can, you put tents and care for it as before.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	And don't go too far in depth, lest you cut the tenant who holds the foundation, and the evacuations will come by chance without intention.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	Then care for it as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	By chance if it is sound, or you remove that covering and clean it since it has been cut near the foundation, by tent or by another appointed instrument.
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	Then cleanse that flesh which is in the wound, as much as you can.
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	Then study to restore the wound and to keep the fistula in the part beyond the foundation:
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	if it is a lighter thing for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And some times fistulas are according to this manner:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	and it is when you set up the tent in the fistula, and it is on the outer side of the foundation below the skin above, so take a pierced tent at the head according to this form:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And I put one twisted thread into two, and put the tent all along the thread in the fistula until it reaches the head.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is torn in the margin of the foundation inside, then pull out the thread from that perforation, so that you set your tent or foundation;
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	and draw the head of the thread, and tie together the two ends together, and hold one to the other, and let it be for one day or two;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and restrain it occasionally, until the threads have worked their way through what is between them, and separate;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then treat the wound until it is closed and healed.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not pierce, then make it pierce in all ways that you can, except if it is too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not necessary to cut too far down and then cure, as we have said, until it is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The form of the spaticular spine from which one makes a fistula is very rough, one side and jagged;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and on the other side not, because of which it does not cut at all that which one should not cut at all, as you see here:
des emorroydes	of hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	Dislocations are according to two manners:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	where they are within the foundation, like grains of resin, and there are small and large ones, and in court blood comes, and there is one or multiple, and they go outside the foundation and to the top of the foundation;
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	but those that are outside have little moisture, and in court or a little yellow water or a little blood, and they have the color of the flesh;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	and the cure for those who have them within the foundation is that you instruct the patient to stretch and lie down in chambers until the foundations come out, and then the sons appear;
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	so hasten, and take it with pincers, or hold it to your nail, then cut into its roots;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if the ligaments cannot hold them because of their moisture, then take them with a cloth, or cotton, or a piece of camlet;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	and strain them to your fingers, then chop, and powder on some hot powders that are in place of cauterize;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or you cauterize them as it is said or chapter of cauterize, then cure other wounds until they are healed;
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the foundations cannot come out, then purgative him with a biting and harsh purge to cleanse what is in the foundation, so that it may come out openly;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	when the patient becomes inflamed, and if the thread is pulled too far from the foundation, then the treatment is light;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	and that you grasp them with your finger or with pincers, and chop, then cure as we have said, until he is healed, and so that he fears the incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	It is necessary that you bring the stitching in this manner:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	Take I twisted thread, and insert it into a needle, then draw the thread above and make the needle pierce from the other side, and turn the two ends of the thread under the needle, so that it is of width.
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and tighten the thread firmly, then tie the thread, and pull out the needle, and do this with all the others, and leave one for correcting the excess of blood.
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	then place a damp cloth soaked in oil or cerot on the foundation, and place it on the foundation, and instruct the patient to rest.
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then let him be until he has purged, and when they are purged, so treat him with ointment and other treatments, until he is healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	of the dryness of the fiend or foundation
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times it happens that dryness of the intestines occurs, and due to constriction of nature, and when the patient is old and medicine does not help.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	It is necessary that you cut at the tip of a spatula or with your fingernail the scab above, which does not let it moisten.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	then care for him as long as he is sick as necessary;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	and if he cannot recover, then resurface the sore even stronger than before until he heals a little and is purged;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then care for him as long as he is healed.
dou fremit	of the shivering
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	A fungus is a small imperfection located outside the body and goes very deep;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	and sometimes it freezes through to the bone, and one feels it as much as dead of numbness, and comes throughout the body, and more in the arms than elsewhere.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment is that you take a goose quill or a strong peacock feather and place it on the numbness, until the circles purple the numbness entirely.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	then turn your hand all around the quill until you cover entirely the numbness, and put it deep inside, and draw out the numbness from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see, then do this with a file of iron or steel in this form, and be subtle below and drawing above.
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	not to pierce, but rather to hold firm at two, and to press.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	And if you see, then cauterize the tremor, as it is written before or in this chapter of cauterization.
de la forme dou clistere	of the form of a purgative
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	One never makes a poultice with silver or archaut, or melted tin or maillet;
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	and one never makes any of these small and great instruments, according to the method by which they are prepared.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Those then which are used in the care of children and those who are weak and painful are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of a purgative small and great is thus broad or the belly is bound in this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	and if there is a deviation or the bowels are tied, as you see, and the head inside pierced;
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	and it has two holes on one side and one on the other.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	and the bowels are tied with medicines from a deer's bladder or parchment, and pierced all around by small holes, and has between each hole one span of distance, then pour in these holes one strong thread twisted in X or eight times around, and assemble the belly as if it were a kid.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	and when the medicine is inside, bind it to the instrument with a strong thread, then cleanse.
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	and this is the shape of a circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine not be too hot nor too cold, and anoint the head of the clyster with oil or egg white or something similar, then fill it lightly.
